2024-10-18 07:41:14====>获取就诊信息:Select Decode(B.急诊,1,'2','1') As visitTypeCode,A.ID As visitNo,to_char(A.开始时间,'yyyymmdd') As visitDate,
                                   C.编码 As deptCode,C.简称 As deptName,'' As wardCode,'' As wardName,'' As bedNo,
                                   D.编码 As doctorId,D.姓名 As doctorName,D.身份证号 As doctorIdentityNo
                              From 服务活动记录 A,个人挂号记录 B,部门 C,医护人员 D
                             Where A.Id=B.记录id And A.科室id=C.资源id And A.服务人id=D.资源id
                               And A.id='AF707BEE-8808-48C9-99E3-DC65E66B678D'

                                   C.编码 As deptCode,C.简称 As deptName,E.编码 As wardCode,E.简称 As wardName,B.床号 As bedNo,
                                   D.编码 As doctorId,D.姓名 As doctorName,D.身份证号 As doctorIdentityNo
                              From 服务活动记录 A,个人入院记录 B,部门 C,医护人员 D,部门 E

                               And A.id='AF707BEE-8808-48C9-99E3-DC65E66B678D'

2024-10-18 09:01:45====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = '93f8007a-e944-4800-a169-7546275cb0bf'
                            And a.事件id = '24B56A56-8732-6F4D-E064-9CDC71ADEB60'
                            And a.组序号 in (14)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-10-18 09:01:45====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = '93f8007a-e944-4800-a169-7546275cb0bf'
                            And a.事件id = '24B56A56-8732-6F4D-E064-9CDC71ADEB60'
                            And a.组序号 in (15)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-10-18 09:09:21====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = '54813a74-0dd1-4dd4-857c-6d332d588c2f'
                            And a.事件id = '9EDB95A0-E9E9-4C60-A38E-3C56D9766C9F'
                            And a.组序号 in (10)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-10-18 09:32:05====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'BDA242D7-6D1C-13A2-E054-9CDC71ADEEF6'
                            And a.事件id = '24B5B810-0039-0455-E064-9CDC71ADEB60'
                            And a.组序号 in (12)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-10-18 09:32:06====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'BDA242D7-6D1C-13A2-E054-9CDC71ADEEF6'
                            And a.事件id = '24B5B810-0039-0455-E064-9CDC71ADEB60'
                            And a.组序号 in (14)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-10-18 09:32:06====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'BDA242D7-6D1C-13A2-E054-9CDC71ADEEF6'
                            And a.事件id = '24B5B810-0039-0455-E064-9CDC71ADEB60'
                            And a.组序号 in (16)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-10-18 09:42:34====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = '8a756e3d-8867-4bb9-a236-6e2e62500d49'
                            And a.事件id = 'B9AF28E4-277A-4483-8FBE-6B06A7C34A77'
                            And a.组序号 in (14)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-10-18 09:42:34====>获取就诊信息:Select B.编码 As visit_departments,B.简称 As visit_departments_name,'1' As visit_type,A.Id As visit_no,'' As ward_code,'' As ward_name,'' As bed_no,nvl(D.保险号,'-') As medical_insurance_number
                          From 服务活动记录 A,部门 B,保险个人档案 D
                         Where A.Id='B9AF28E4-277A-4483-8FBE-6B06A7C34A77'
                           And A.科室id=B.资源id And A.个人id=D.个人id(+)
                           And A.项目id='F4DA8ED2-5033-47EB-A08F-E442A5E65DAB'
                        Union All
                        Select B.编码 As visit_departments,B.简称 As visit_departments_name,'3' As visit_type,A.Id As visit_no,E.编码 As ward_code,E.简称 As ward_name,C.床号 As bed_no,nvl(D.保险号,'-') As medical_insurance_number
                          From 服务活动记录 A,部门 B,保险个人档案 D,个人当前状态 C,部门 E
                         Where A.Id='B9AF28E4-277A-4483-8FBE-6B06A7C34A77'
                           And A.科室id=B.资源id And A.个人id=D.个人id(+) And A.Id=C.就诊id And C.病房id=E.资源id
                           And A.项目id='EC3E41BF-BACD-46BA-9D3C-E2493D73C1DF'
2024-10-18 09:42:34====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = '8a756e3d-8867-4bb9-a236-6e2e62500d49'
                            And a.事件id = 'B9AF28E4-277A-4483-8FBE-6B06A7C34A77'
                            And a.组序号 in (16)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = '54813a74-0dd1-4dd4-857c-6d332d588c2f'
                            And a.事件id = '9EDB95A0-E9E9-4C60-A38E-3C56D9766C9F'
                            And a.组序号 in (22)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-10-18 12:03:25====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = '4f2d7523-000f-4e3a-ba71-e06c2e592076'
                            And a.事件id = '24B8139E-7C87-2B03-E064-9CDC71ADEEF6'
                            And a.组序号 in (14)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-10-18 12:03:26====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = '4f2d7523-000f-4e3a-ba71-e06c2e592076'
                            And a.事件id = '24B8139E-7C87-2B03-E064-9CDC71ADEEF6'
                            And a.组序号 in (16)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-10-18 14:57:31====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'BDA242DA-66B1-13A2-E054-9CDC71ADEEF6'
                            And a.事件id = '24BA798C-03D2-3D53-E064-9CDC71ADEEF6'
                            And a.组序号 in (13)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'BDA242DA-66B1-13A2-E054-9CDC71ADEEF6'
                            And a.事件id = '24BA798C-03D2-3D53-E064-9CDC71ADEEF6'
                            And a.组序号 in (15)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'BDA242DA-66B1-13A2-E054-9CDC71ADEEF6'
                            And a.事件id = '24BA798C-03D2-3D53-E064-9CDC71ADEEF6'
                            And a.组序号 in (26)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-10-18 19:17:33====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'BDA242D7-8B17-13A2-E054-9CDC71ADEEF6'
                            And a.事件id = 'AF707BEE-8808-48C9-99E3-DC65E66B678D'
                            And a.组序号 in (76)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-10-18 21:52:27====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'BDA242D5-B6CC-13A2-E054-9CDC71ADEEF6'
                            And a.事件id = '24C085D6-5185-3C34-E064-9CDC71ADEB60'
                            And a.组序号 in (1)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-10-18 22:20:51====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'BDA242D5-B6CC-13A2-E054-9CDC71ADEEF6'
                            And a.事件id = '24C085D6-5185-3C34-E064-9CDC71ADEB60'
                            And a.组序号 in (15)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-10-18 22:20:51====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'BDA242D5-B6CC-13A2-E054-9CDC71ADEEF6'
                            And a.事件id = '24C085D6-5185-3C34-E064-9CDC71ADEB60'
                            And a.组序号 in (16)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno
